PA, DE'I DBUS SU YANG GRU GSUM PA STE, RDO RJE RTZE GSUM PA'I
PHRENG BAS YONGS SU BSKOR BA 'DI'I DBUS SU YANG MTSAN MA BYA STE,
STAG DANG SBRUL DANG SENG GE RNAMS KYI GDONG PA GANG 'DOD PAS
MTSAN MAR BYA

ZHING MAR 'DZAG PA'I BU GA SOR GCIG PA'O, ,MCHU NI RDO RJE GDENG
PA 'DAR BAS BYIN GYIS BRLABS PA'I SOR TSAD TZAM MO, ,DE BZHIN DU
BLUGS GZAR GYI YU BA NI SOR BCU BZHI PA DKYUS SOR GSUM PA, ZABS
SOR GCIG PA GRU GSUM PA DE BZHIN DU MTSAN MAS BYIN GYIS

BRLABS PA'O, ,YU BA'I MTHAR NI RDO RJE RTZE GSUM GDENGS PAS BYIN
GYIS RLABS PA'I MNGON SPYOD KYI GZAR BU DGANG BAR BYA STE, THOG
GIS BRGYAB PA'I SHING NGAM LCAGS SAM, TSER MA RNO BA CAN GYI SHING
RNAMS LAS BYA'O, ,'DIS NI SANGS RGYAS DAG KYANG NGES PAR

'JIG ZHES BYA PA'I DON NO, ,DE LTAR PHYI ROL GYI SPYIN SREG BSHAD
NAS, YANG NANG GI BSTAN PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, SNGAGS DANG PHYAG RGYA
YANG DAG LDAN, ,DPA' BO RNAMS KYI ZAS DE BZHIN, ,ZHES BYA BA
GSUNGS TE, SNGON DU BSTAN PA'I RDZAS RNAMS KYIS, ,RANG GI LHAG
BA'I LHA'I SBYOR

@54A *, ,BA DANG LDAN PAS BYA'O, ,NYON MONGS THAMS CAD ZHI DON
DANG, ,TING NGE 'DZIN NI RGYAS BYA'I PHYIR, ,SRID GSUM SNYING
PO'I THAB KHUNG DU, ,LAS RNAMS THAMS CAD RAB BSGRUB BYA, ,RANG
BZHIN GYIS BYUNG LTE BA RU, ,GTUM MO'I ME NI BZANG POS BRGYAN,
,RTZA BA'I RANG

BZHIN HE RU KA ,RNAL 'BYOR PA KUN DGANG BAR BYA, ,RANG BZHIN MED
PA'I SEMS KYIS NI, ,'BYUNG BA KUN GYI SREG BLUGS BYA, ,'DI NI BLA
MED SBYIN SREG TU, ,SANGS RGYAS KUN GYIS RAB TU GSUNGS, ,RANG GIS
BDAG NYID RANG BZHIN DU, ,PHYI YI DNGOS PO SHES BAR BYA, ,DE LTAR

YANG GSUNGS PA, 'OD ZER PHRENG BAS 'KHRIGS SHING DRAG ,'OD KYI
DKYIL 'KHOR RAB 'BAR BA, ,LTE BA'I THAB KHUNG KUN DU GSUNGS, ,LTE
BA ME YI THAB KHUNG NYID, ,BUD SHING THAMS CAD YE SHES MES,
,'BYIN DANG SDUD PAR BYED PA YIN, ,LAS KYI RLUNG GIS RAB BSKYOD
PAS, ,LTE BA'I

DKYIL DU RAB TU 'BAR, ,DBANG PO KUN LAS BYUNG BA'I SEMS, ,BDE BA
BUD SHING DU NI 'GYUR, ,LAS DANG SKYE BA LAS BYUNG BA, ,NYON MONGS
ZHI PHYIR SBYIN SREG BYA, ,RDZOGS PA'I BYANG CHUB RIM GYIS NI,
,'DI YIS MYUR DU RGYAS PAR 'GYUR, ,BSKAL PA'I ME DANG RTOGS
MTSUNGS

SHING; ,'OD KYI SNANG BAS LEGS GNAS PA, ,RTZA BRGYAD RNAMS KYI
'BRAS BU NI, ,SNYING GA'I GNAS SU YANG DGA' BAR, ,DRUG CU RTZA
BZHI'I 'DAB LDAN PA'I, ,PADMA NYID KYI DBUS SU ME, ,DE YI DBUS SU
ME YI LHA, ,MTHE BO'I TSIGS TSAD TZAM DU BLTA, ,PHYAG GNYIS ME YI

MDOG CAN MA, ,LHAN CIG SKYES DGA' RAB 'BAR BA'I, ,NYI MA'I DKYIL
'KHOR MNAN NAS NI, ,'OD ZER 'BAR BAS RAB GSAL BA, ,DBYINGS KUN LA
NI 'BAR BYED PA, ,THAMS CAD RTZA RU SONG BAR BLTA, ,BLTA BA KUN
GYI BUD SHING NI, ,'DAB MA'I MTHAR NI YANG DAG GSUNGS, ,

YID KYIS ME TOG MCHOD BYA ZHING, ,YID KYIS BDUG PAS BDUG PAR BYA,
,YID KYI DRI NI BDE DANG LDAN, ,YID KYI MAR ME RAB 'BAR BA, ,GTOR
MA 'DUS BYAS GANG BA YI, ,YID NYID KYIS NI MCHOD PAR BYA, ,RKYANG
MA DGANG GZAR YANG DAG GSUNGS, ,RO BCUD

GNYIS TSAD DU RAB RGYAS PA'O, ,DBYUG PA RDO RJE RIN CHEN MTHA',

,THAMS CAD RDZAS NI SREG BLUGS BYAS, ,DE LTAR RIM PA RAB TU
BRJOD, ,RTZA LNGA

LA NI YANG DAG BRTEN, ,LNGA PO YANG DAG SBYAR BAR BYA, ,SA DANG

KHYAB BYED GNAS PA STE, ,MKHAS PAS KUN TU BSKOR BAR BYA, ,'DAB
BRGYAD

BA YIS, ,BDUD RTZI'I YI GE YANG DAG LDAN, ,BDUD RTZI DKYIL 'KHOR

BAL GYI SDONG PU

SHES SNANG BYED PA, ,SBAS PA'I NYI MA'I ZHAL SNGA NAS, ,LA WA PA
YIS DKA' 'GREL NI, ,'BAD PA CHEN POS BSHAD PA'O, ,RGYA GAR GYI
MKHAN PO S'U RYA GUPTA DANG, BOD KYI LO TZ'A BA 'GOS LHAS BTZAS
KYIS BSGYUR CING ZHUS TE GTAN LA PHAB PA'O,, ,,
